<script>
	csv_data = new Array();
	csv_received = false;
	cur_page = 1;
	max_page = 1;
	per_page = 50;
	str_prev_page = ""
	str_next_page = ""
	url_raw = "https://fgo.wiki/w/SVT";
	url_display = "/w/英灵图鉴";
	f1_names = ["class", "stars", "cards", "np-color", "np-type", "method", "process"];
	f2_names = ["sex", "prop1", "prop2", "fac", "traits"];
	clip_board = null;
	params_str = location.search.replace(/%2F/g, "").replace(/\//g, "");
	body_loaded = false;

	isMobile = is_mobile();
	if (isMobile)
	{
		str_prev_page = "◀";
		str_next_page = "▶";
		document.getElementById("whole_frame").removeChild(document.getElementById("desktop_filter"));
		document.getElementById("mobile_filter").style.display = "";
	}
	else
	{
		str_prev_page = "◀上一页";
		str_next_page = "下一页▶";
		document.getElementById("whole_frame").removeChild(document.getElementById("mobile_filter"));
		document.getElementById("desktop_filter").style.display = "";
	}
	
	pre_load()

	function filter_class_onlick(c)
	{
		var img_btn = document.getElementById(c);
		img_btn.setAttribute("enabled", 1 - img_btn.getAttribute("enabled"));
		apply_filters();
	}
	function filter_allclasses_onlick(c)
	{
		var new_value = c;
		
		var class_filters = document.getElementById("filter-class").getElementsByTagName("img");
		for (var i = 0; i < class_filters.length; i++)
		{
			if (class_filters[i].hasAttribute("enabled")) class_filters[i].setAttribute("enabled", new_value);
		}

		apply_filters();
	}
	function filter_selectall_onlick(cur_btn, field, new_value)
	{
		var cur_filters = document.getElementById(field).getElementsByTagName("input");
		for (var i = 0; i < cur_filters.length; i++)
		{
			if (cur_filters[i].hasAttribute("bit")) cur_filters[i].checked = new_value;
		}
		
		apply_filters();
	}
	function clear_filter1()
	{
		for (var k = 0; k < f1_names.length; k++)
		{
			var p_name = f1_names[k];
			if (p_name == "class") continue;
			
			var filters = document.getElementById("filter-" + p_name).getElementsByTagName("input");
			for (var i = 0; i < filters.length; i++)
			{
				if (filters[i].hasAttribute("bit")) filters[i].checked = false;
			}
		}
		filter_allclasses_onlick(0);
	}
	function clear_filter2()
	{
		for (var k = 0; k < f2_names.length; k++)
		{
			var p_name = f2_names[k];
			var filters = document.getElementById("filter-" + p_name).getElementsByTagName("input");
			for (var i = 0; i < filters.length; i++)
			{
				if (filters[i].hasAttribute("bit")) filters[i].checked = false;
			}
		}
		document.getElementById("filter-traits-modand").checked = false;
		document.getElementById("filter-traits-modnot").checked = false;
		apply_filters();
	}

	function copyURL(btn)
	{
		if (!clip_board) return;
		var copyText = document.getElementById("list-filter-url").innerHTML.replace(/&amp;/g, "&");
		btn.setAttribute("data-clipboard-text", copyText);
		alert("链接已复制: " + copyText);
	}
	function table_header(icon_mode)
	{
		if (icon_mode)
			return isMobile? "\t<table class=\"wikitable\" style=\"text-align:left;margin:0;min-width:100%;table-layout:fixed;display:table;white-space:normal;\"><tr><td>\n" : "\t<table class=\"wikitable\" style=\"text-align:left;margin:0;min-width:100%;table-layout:fixed;display:table;\"><tr><td>\n";
		else
			return isMobile? "\t<table class=\"wikitable\" id=\"lancelot_table_mobile_servantlist\" style=\"text-align:center;margin:0;min-width:100%;table-layout:fixed;display:table;white-space:normal;font-size:unset;\">" : "\t<table class=\"wikitable\" id=\"lancelot_table_servantlist\" style=\"text-align:center;margin:0;min-width:100%;table-layout:fixed;display:table;\">\n\t\t<tr class=\"column-header\">\n\t\t\t<th>No.</th>\n\t\t\t<th>头像</th>\n\t\t\t<th>姓名</th>\n\t\t\t<th>宝具</th>\n\t\t\t<th>职阶</th>\n\t\t\t<th>配卡</th>\n\t\t\t<th>属性</th>\n\t\t\t<th>获取途径</th>\n\t\t\t<th>满级ATK</th>\n\t\t\t<th>满级HP</th>\n\t\t</tr>";
	}
	function table_tail(icon_mode)
	{
		if (icon_mode)
			return "\n\t</td></tr></table>";
		else
			return "\t</table>";
	}
	function display_servant(i, icon_mode)
	{
		var subpage = "";
		if (icon_mode)
		{
			var icon_width = isMobile ? "20%" : "10%";
			table_str += "<div style=\"width:" + icon_width + ";display:inline-block;\"><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_link) + subpage + "\"><img style=\"width:96%;padding:2%;\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].avatar) +"\" onerror=\"this.src='/images/1/13/未知技能.png';this.onerror=null\"></" + "a></" + "div>";
		}
		else
		{
			var collectable = (csv_data[i - 1].card1 != "");
			if(!isMobile)
			{
				table_str += "\t\t<tr>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].id) + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_link) + subpage + "\"><img style=\"height:81px\" src=\""+ htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].avatar) + "\" onerror=\"this.src='/images/1/13/未知技能.png';this.onerror=null\"></a></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_link) + subpage + "\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_cn) + "</a><br><span lang=\"ja\" style=\"font-size:x-small;\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_jp) + "</span><br><span style=\"font-size:x-small;\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_en) + "</span></td>\n";
				table_str += collectable ? "\t\t\t<td><img style=\"height:55px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].np_card) + "\"><br><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].np_type) + "</b></td>\n" : "\t\t\t<td></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].class_link) + "\"><img style=\"height:40px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].class_icon) + "\"></a></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td>\n";
				if (collectable)
				{
					table_str += "\t\t\t\t<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card1) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card2) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card3) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card4) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card5) + "\">\n";
				}
				table_str += "\t\t\t</td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].faction) + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].get).split("&amp;").join("<br>") + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].atk) + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].hp) + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t</tr>\n";
			}
			else
			{
				table_str += " \t\t<tr>\n";
				table_str += collectable ? "\t\t\t<td rowspan=\"2\"><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].id) + "</b></td>\n" : "\t\t\t<td><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].id) + "</b></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_link) + subpage + "\"><img style=\"width:80px\" src=\""+ htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].avatar) + "\" onerror=\"this.src='/images/1/13/未知技能.png';this.onerror=null\"></a></td>\n";
				table_str +=  "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_link) + subpage + "\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_cn) + "</a><br><span lang=\"ja\" style=\"font-size:x-small;\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_jp) + "</span><br><span style=\"font-size:x-small;\">" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].name_en) + "</span></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t\t<td><a href=\"/w/" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].class_link) + "\"><img style=\"width:40px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].class_icon) + "\"></a></td>\n";
				table_str += "\t\t</tr>\n";
				if (collectable)
				{
					table_str += "\t\t<tr>\n";
					table_str += "\t\t\t<td><img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].np_card) + "\"><b>" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].np_type) + "</b></td>\n";
					table_str += "\t\t\t<td colspan=\"2\">\n";
					table_str += "\t\t\t\t<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card1) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card2) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card3) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card4) + "\">";
					table_str += "<img style=\"height:35px\" src=\"" + htmlEncode(csv_data[i - 1].card5) + "\">\n";
					table_str += "\t\t\t</td>\n";
					table_str += "\t\t</tr> \n";
				}
			}
		}
	}
	function get_process_status(id, mask)
	{
		//var one_in_54 = [3, 5, 6, 10, 11, 14, 18, 29, 30, 41, 46, 47, 48, 58, 66, 67, 74, 78, 82, 87, 89, 94, 100, 101, 102, 103, 109, 116, 120, 121, 122, 123, 140, 145, 146, 147, 157, 158, 159, 165, 170, 171, 183, 184, 185, 187, 188, 192, 193, 194, 202, 207, 214, 223];
		var one_in_60 = [3, 5, 6, 10, 11, 14, 18, 29, 30, 41, 46, 47, 48, 58, 66, 67, 74, 78, 82, 87, 89, 94, 100, 101, 102, 103, 109, 116, 120, 121, 122, 123, 140, 145, 146, 147, 157, 158, 159, 165, 170, 171, 183, 184, 185, 187, 188, 192, 193, 194, 202, 207, 214, 223, 227, 228, 230, 242, 245, 248];
		var one_in_ssr = [2, 8, 37, 52, 59, 60, 62, 65, 75, 76, 84, 85, 97, 113, 118, 143, 169, 189, 201, 206, 212, 226, 232, 244, 274];
		if ((mask & 4) && (one_in_60.indexOf(id) >= 0)) return true;
        if ((mask & 8) && (one_in_ssr.indexOf(id) >= 0)) return true;
		var is_cn_process = (id <= 274)
		switch(mask & 3)
		{
		case 1:
			return is_cn_process;
		case 2:
			return !is_cn_process;
		case 3:
			return true;
		default:
			return false;
		}
	}
	function search_servant(i, str)
	{
		var csv_datum = csv_data[i - 1];
		var key_words = str.toLowerCase().split(" ");
		var success = true;
		var success_plain = false;
		var n_plain = 0;
		
		for (var j = 0; j < key_words.length; j++)
		{
			if (key_words[j] == "") continue;
			
			var key_word_mode = 0;
			if (key_words[j].charAt(0) == "+")
			{
				key_word_mode = +1;
				key_words[j] = key_words[j].substring(1);
			}
			else if (key_words[j].charAt(0) == "-")
			{
				key_word_mode = -1;
				key_words[j] = key_words[j].substring(1);
			}
			
			var exact_id = (is_str_pure_int(key_words[j]) && key_words[j].charAt(0) == "0");
			
			var success0 = (exact_id ? csv_datum.id == parseInt(key_words[j]).toString() : csv_datum.id.indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_cn.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_cn.toLowerCase().replace(/・/g,"").indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_en.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_jp.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_link.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				(csv_datum.name_other.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1) ||
				("tag" in csv_datum && csv_datum.tag.toLowerCase().indexOf(key_words[j]) != -1);
				
			if (key_word_mode == 0)
			{
				success_plain = success_plain || success0;
				n_plain++;
			}
			else
			{
				success = success && ((key_word_mode == +1) ? success0 : !success0);
			}
		}
		return (n_plain == 0) ? success : (success_plain && success);
	}
	function apply_class_icons()
	{
		var class_mask = 0;
		var class_filters = document.getElementById("filter-class").getElementsByTagName("img");
		for (var i = 0; i < class_filters.length; i++)
		{
			if (!class_filters[i].hasAttribute("enabled")) continue;
			var class_name = class_filters[i].id;
			class_filters[i].src = (class_filters[i].getAttribute("enabled") == 1) ? window[class_name + "_on"] : window[class_name + "_off"];
			if (class_filters[i].getAttribute("bit") != undefined && class_filters[i].getAttribute("enabled") == 1) 
				class_mask |= class_filters[i].getAttribute("bit");
		}
		return class_mask;
	}
	function apply_filters()
	{
		if(!csv_received) return;
		
		var list_old = list_sort_id1;
		var sort_filters = document.getElementById("filter-sort").getElementsByTagName("input");
		var sort_ids = {"filter-sort-id1" : 0, "filter-sort-id0" : 1, "filter-sort-atk1" : 2, "filter-sort-atk0" : 3, "filter-sort-hp1" : 4, "filter-sort-hp0" : 5};
		var sort_seleted = 0;
		for(var i = 0; i < sort_filters.length; i++)
		{
			if (sort_filters[i].id != "iconmode" && sort_filters[i].checked)
			{
				list_old = window["list_sort_" + sort_filters[i].id.substring(12)];
				sort_seleted = sort_ids[sort_filters[i].id];
				break;
			}
		}
		
		var filter_names = f1_names.concat(f2_names);
		list_display = new Array();
		masks = new Object();
		
		masks["class"] = apply_class_icons();
		
		for (var k = 0; k < filter_names.length; k++)
		{
			var p_name = filter_names[k];
			if (p_name == "class") continue;
			
			masks[p_name] = 0;
			var filters = document.getElementById("filter-" + p_name).getElementsByTagName("input");
			for (var i = 0; i < filters.length; i++)
			{
				var btn_bit = filters[i].getAttribute("bit");
				if (btn_bit != undefined && filters[i].checked) masks[p_name] |= btn_bit;
			}
		}
		
		var search_str = document.getElementById("filter-search").value;
		
		var mod_and = document.getElementById("filter-traits-modand").checked
		var mod_not = document.getElementById("filter-traits-modnot").checked
		for (var i = 0; i < list_old.length; i++)
		{
			var csv_datum = csv_data[list_old[i] - 1];
			var is_traits_pass = (!mod_and && (csv_datum.traits_marker & masks["traits"]) > 0) || (mod_and && (csv_datum.traits_marker & masks["traits"]) == masks["traits"]);
			if (
			(masks["class"] == 0 || (csv_datum.class_marker & masks["class"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["stars"] == 0 || (csv_datum.stars_marker & masks["stars"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["cards"] == 0 || (csv_datum.cards_marker & masks["cards"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["np-color"] == 0 || (csv_datum.npc_marker & masks["np-color"]) > 0) > 0 &&
			(masks["np-type"] == 0 || (csv_datum.npt_marker & masks["np-type"]) > 0) > 0 &&
			(masks["method"] == 0 || (csv_datum.get_marker & masks["method"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["sex"] == 0 || (csv_datum.sex_marker & masks["sex"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["prop1"] == 0 || (csv_datum.prop1_marker & masks["prop1"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["prop2"] == 0 || (csv_datum.prop2_marker & masks["prop2"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["fac"] == 0 || (csv_datum.fac_marker & masks["fac"]) > 0) &&
			(masks["process"] == 0 || get_process_status(parseInt(csv_datum.id), masks["process"])) &&
			(masks["traits"] == 0 || is_traits_pass != mod_not) &&
			(search_str == "" || search_servant(list_old[i], search_str))
			) list_display.push(list_old[i]);
		}
		
		refresh_pages();
		
		var class_base64 = int_Base64(masks["class"]);
		var stars_base64 = int_Base64(masks["stars"]);
		var cards_base64 = int_Base64(masks["cards"]);
		var npc_base64 = int_Base64(masks["np-color"]);
		var npt_base64 = int_Base64(masks["np-type"]);
		var method_base64 = int_Base64(masks["method"]);
		var process_base64 = int_Base64(masks["process"]);
		var sex_base64 = int_Base64(masks["sex"]);
		var prop1_base64 = int_Base64(masks["prop1"]);
		var prop2_base64 = int_Base64(masks["prop2"]);
		var fac_base64 = int_Base64(masks["fac"]);
		var traits_base64 = int_Base64((masks["traits"] << 2) + (mod_and ? 2 : 0) + (mod_not ? 1 : 0));
		var search_base64 = utf8_Base64(search_str);
		var sort_base64 = int_Base64(sort_seleted);
		
		var f1_base64 = [class_base64, stars_base64, cards_base64, npc_base64, npt_base64, method_base64, process_base64].join(",");
		var f2_base64 = [sex_base64, prop1_base64, prop2_base64, fac_base64, traits_base64].join(",");
		
		var url_suffix = ""
		if (f1_base64 != ",,,,,,") url_suffix += "&f1=" + f1_base64;
		if (f2_base64 != ",,,,") url_suffix += "&f2=" + f2_base64;
		if (sort_base64 != "") url_suffix += "&px=" + sort_base64;
		if (search_base64 != "") url_suffix += "&ssl=" + search_base64;
		
		if (url_suffix != "") document.getElementById("list-filter-url").innerHTML = url_raw + "?" + url_suffix.substr(1) + "/";
		else document.getElementById("list-filter-url").innerHTML = url_raw;
		
		window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, url_display);
	}
	function refresh_pages()
	{
		per_page = document.getElementById("per-page").value;
		max_page = Math.max(Math.ceil(list_display.length / per_page), 1);
		cur_page = Math.min(max_page, cur_page);
		
		var cur_page_str = ""
		for (var i = 1; i <= max_page; i++)
		{
			cur_page_str += "\t\t\t\t<option value=" + i + ">" + i + "</option>\n"
		}
		document.getElementById("cur-page").innerHTML = cur_page_str;
		document.getElementById("cur-page-bottom").innerHTML = cur_page_str;
		
		set_page();
	}
	function set_page()
	{
		document.getElementById("PrevPage").style.visibility = (cur_page == 1) ? "hidden" : "visible";
		document.getElementById("PrevPage-bottom").style.visibility = (cur_page == 1) ? "hidden" : "visible";
		document.getElementById("NextPage").style.visibility = (cur_page == max_page) ? "hidden" : "visible";
		document.getElementById("NextPage-bottom").style.visibility = (cur_page == max_page) ? "hidden" : "visible";
		document.getElementById("cur-page").options[cur_page - 1].selected = true;
		document.getElementById("cur-page-bottom").options[cur_page - 1].selected = true;
		document.getElementById("PageInfo").innerHTML = "共" + list_display.length + "条";
		var icon_mode = document.getElementById("iconmode").checked;

		table_str = table_header(icon_mode);
		if (list_display.length == 0)
		{
			table_str += isMobile ? "\t\t<tr><td>没有结果</td></tr>\n\t</table>" : "\t\t<tr>\n\t\t\t<td colspan=\"10\">没有结果</td>\n\t\t</tr>\n";
		}
		else
		{
			first = (cur_page - 1) * per_page + 1;
			last = Math.min(cur_page * per_page, list_display.length);
//			document.getElementById("PageInfo").innerHTML = "共" + list_display.length + "条，现显示" + first + "~" + last;
			for (var i = first; i <= last; i++)
			{
				display_servant(list_display[i - 1], icon_mode);
			}
		}

		table_str += table_tail(icon_mode);
		document.getElementById("list").innerHTML = table_str;
	}
 
	function get_url_params()
	{
		var url_params = GetQueryString(params_str);
		if (Object.keys(url_params).length == 0) return;
		
		var filter_names = f1_names.concat(f2_names);
		if ("ssl" in url_params) url_params["ssl"] = Base64_utf8(Base64_UrlDecode(url_params["ssl"]));
		if ("px" in url_params) url_params["px"] = Base64_int(Base64_UrlDecode(url_params["px"]));
		if ("f1" in url_params) url_params["f1"] = Base64_UrlDecode(url_params["f1"]);
		if ("f2" in url_params) url_params["f2"] = Base64_UrlDecode(url_params["f2"]);

		var filter_btns = new Object();
		
		filter_btns["class_btns"] = new Object();
		var class_filters = document.getElementById("filter-class").getElementsByTagName("img");
		for (var i = 0; i < class_filters.length; i++)
		{
			if (!class_filters[i].hasAttribute("enabled")) continue;
			
			var btn_bit = class_filters[i].getAttribute("bit")
			if (btn_bit != undefined) filter_btns["class_btns"][btn_bit] = class_filters[i];
		}
		
		for (var k = 0; k < filter_names.length; k++)
		{
			var p_name = filter_names[k];
			if (p_name == "class") continue;
			
			filter_btns[p_name + "_btns"] = new Object();
			var filters = document.getElementById("filter-" + p_name).getElementsByTagName("input");
			for (var i = 0; i < filters.length; i++)
			{
				var btn_bit = filters[i].getAttribute("bit")
				if (btn_bit != undefined) filter_btns[p_name + "_btns"][btn_bit] = filters[i];
			}
		}
		
		if ("f1" in url_params && url_params["f1"] != ",,,,,,")
		{
			var f1_params = url_params["f1"].split(",");
			
			if (f1_params[0] != undefined && f1_params[0] != "")
			{
				var mask = Base64_int(f1_params[0]);
				var btns = filter_btns["class_btns"];
				for (bit in btns) btns[bit].setAttribute("enabled", ((mask & bit) != 0) ? 1 : 0);
				apply_class_icons();
			}
			
			for (var i = 1; i < f1_names.length; i++)
			{
				if (f1_params[i] != undefined && f1_params[i] != "")
				{
					var mask = Base64_int(f1_params[i]);
					var btns = filter_btns[f1_names[i] + "_btns"];
					for (bit in btns) btns[bit].checked = ((mask & bit) != 0);
				}
			}
			document.getElementById("filter1").className = "wikitable mw-collapsible";
		}
		if ("f2" in url_params && url_params["f2"] != ",,,,")
		{
			var f2_params = url_params["f2"].split(",");
			for (var i = 0; i < f2_names.length; i++)
			{
				if (f2_params[i] != undefined && f2_params[i] != "")
				{
					var mask = Base64_int(f2_params[i]);
					if (f2_names[i] == "traits")
					{
						document.getElementById("filter-traits-modnot").checked = ((mask & 1) != 0);
						document.getElementById("filter-traits-modand").checked = ((mask & 2) != 0);
						mask = (mask >> 2);
					}
					var btns = filter_btns[f2_names[i] + "_btns"];
					for (bit in btns) btns[bit].checked = ((mask & bit) != 0);
				}
			}
			document.getElementById("filter2").className = "wikitable mw-collapsible";
		}
		
		if ("ssl" in url_params && url_params["ssl"] != "")
		{
			document.getElementById("filter-search").value = url_params["ssl"];
		}
		if ("px" in url_params && url_params["px"] >= 0)
		{
			var sort_ids = ["filter-sort-id1", "filter-sort-id0", "filter-sort-atk1", "filter-sort-atk0", "filter-sort-hp1", "filter-sort-hp0"];
			document.getElementById(sort_ids[url_params["px"]]).checked = true;
		}
	}
	get_url_params();

		csv_data = table_parser(raw_str, ",");
		list_sort_id0 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		list_sort_id1 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		list_sort_hp0 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		list_sort_hp1 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		list_sort_atk0 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		list_sort_atk1 = new Array(csv_data.length);
		
		var n_uncol = 0;
		for (var i = 0; i < csv_data.length; i++)
		{
			if (csv_data[i].card1 == "") n_uncol++;
			list_sort_id0[i] = i + 1;
			list_sort_id1[i] = csv_data.length - i;
			list_sort_hp0[csv_data[i]["sort_hp"] - 1] = i + 1;
			list_sort_atk0[csv_data[i]["sort_atk"] - 1] = i + 1;
		}
		
		var n_col = csv_data.length - n_uncol;
		for (var i = 0; i < n_col; i++)
		{
			list_sort_hp1[i] = list_sort_hp0[n_col - 1 - i];
			list_sort_atk1[i] = list_sort_atk0[n_col - 1 - i];
		}
		for (var i = n_col; i < csv_data.length; i++)
		{
			list_sort_hp1[i] = list_sort_hp0[i];
			list_sort_atk1[i] = list_sort_atk0[i];
		}
		
		extra_data(override_data);
		
		csv_received = true;
		apply_filters();
		
		clip_board = new ClipboardJS('#list-filter-url-copy');
    }
    
    svt_type_str_to_marker = {"未知": 0, "初始获得": 1, "事前登录赠送": 2, "活动赠送": 4, "通关报酬": 8, "友情点召唤": 16, "圣晶石常驻": 32, "剧情限定": 64, "期间限定": 128, "无法获得": 256};
	function extra_data(data)
	{
        var curr_id = 0;
        var data_list = data.split("\n");
		for (var i = 0; i < data_list.length; i++)
		{
            var raw_str = data_list[i].replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g,"");

            var splitter = raw_str.indexOf("=");
            if (splitter == -1) continue;

            var key = raw_str.substring(0, splitter).replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g,"");
            var val = raw_str.substring(splitter + 1).replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g,"");

            if (key == "id")
            {
                var id = parseInt(val);
                if (id <= 0 || id > csv_data.length) continue;
                curr_id = id;
                continue;
            }

            if (curr_id == 0) continue;
            
            if (key == "method")
            {
                csv_data[id - 1]["get"] = val;

                var marker = 0;
                var type_list = val.split("<br>");
                for (var j = 0; j < type_list.length; j++) marker += svt_type_str_to_marker[type_list[j]];
                csv_data[id - 1]["get_marker"] = marker;
            }
			if (key != "name_cn" && key != "name_jp" && key != "name_en" && key != "name_link" && key != "tag" && key != "name_other") continue;
			csv_data[id - 1][key] = val;
        }
	}
</script>

function body_onresize()
{
	var input_width = (document.getElementById("filter2").offsetWidth - 4) + "px";
	document.getElementById("filter-search").style.width = input_width;
	//document.getElementById("list-filter-url").style.width = input_width;
}
function body_onload()
{
	body_onresize();
	window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, url_display);
	body_loaded = true;
}
